    [Project1].[usu_nom_usuario] AS [usu_nom_usuario], 
    [Project1].[usu_nom_login] AS [usu_nom_login], 
    [Project1].[usu_num_senha] AS [usu_num_senha], 
    [Project1].[usu_flg_ativo] AS [usu_flg_ativo], 
    [Project1].[usu_id_gru] AS [usu_id_gru], 
    [Project1].[usu_id_set] AS [usu_id_set], 
    [Project1].[usu_dat_ultimo_acesso] AS [usu_dat_ultimo_acesso], 
    [Project1].[usu_dat_cadastro] AS [usu_dat_cadastro], 
    [Project1].[usu_cod_agenda] AS [usu_cod_agenda]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_usu] AS [usu_id_usu], 
        [Extent1].[usu_uui_identificador] AS [usu_uui_identificador], 
        [Extent1].[usu_nom_usuario] AS [usu_nom_usuario], 
        [Extent1].[usu_nom_login] AS [usu_nom_login], 
        [Extent1].[usu_num_senha] AS [usu_num_senha], 
        [Extent1].[usu_flg_ativo] AS [usu_flg_ativo], 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_gru] AS [usu_id_gru], 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_set] AS [usu_id_set], 
        [Extent1].[usu_dat_ultimo_acesso] AS [usu_dat_ultimo_acesso], 
        [Extent1].[usu_dat_cadastro] AS [usu_dat_cadastro], 
        [Extent1].[usu_cod_agenda] AS [usu_cod_agenda]
        FROM [dbo].[usu_usuario] AS [Extent1]
        WHERE ([Extent1].[usu_nom_usuario] LIKE @p__linq__0 ESCAPE '~') OR ([Extent1].[usu_nom_login] LIKE @p__linq__1 ESCAPE '~')
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY row_number() OVER (ORDER BY [Project1].[usu_dat_cadastro] DESC)
    OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 10 ROWS ONLY

    [Project1].[usu_nom_login] AS [usu_nom_login], 
    [Project1].[usu_num_senha] AS [usu_num_senha], 
    [Project1].[usu_flg_ativo] AS [usu_flg_ativo], 
    [Project1].[usu_id_gru] AS [usu_id_gru], 
    [Project1].[usu_id_set] AS [usu_id_set], 
    [Project1].[usu_dat_ultimo_acesso] AS [usu_dat_ultimo_acesso], 
    [Project1].[usu_dat_cadastro] AS [usu_dat_cadastro], 
    [Project1].[usu_cod_agenda] AS [usu_cod_agenda]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_usu] AS [usu_id_usu], 
        [Extent1].[usu_uui_identificador] AS [usu_uui_identificador], 
        [Extent1].[usu_nom_usuario] AS [usu_nom_usuario], 
        [Extent1].[usu_nom_login] AS [usu_nom_login], 
        [Extent1].[usu_num_senha] AS [usu_num_senha], 
        [Extent1].[usu_flg_ativo] AS [usu_flg_ativo], 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_gru] AS [usu_id_gru], 
        [Extent1].[usu_id_set] AS [usu_id_set], 
        [Extent1].[usu_dat_ultimo_acesso] AS [usu_dat_ultimo_acesso], 
        [Extent1].[usu_dat_cadastro] AS [usu_dat_cadastro], 
        [Extent1].[usu_cod_agenda] AS [usu_cod_agenda]
        FROM [dbo].[usu_usuario] AS [Extent1]
        WHERE ([Extent1].[usu_nom_usuario] LIKE @p__linq__0 ESCAPE '~') OR ([Extent1].[usu_nom_login] LIKE @p__linq__1 ESCAPE '~')
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY row_number() OVER (ORDER BY [Project1].[usu_nom_login] DESC)
    OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 10 ROWS ONLY
